Modified Python tests (1): `test_format_dbc.py` тАФ assertions reflect canonical Agda formatter output (`(.0,)` decimal trail, `BU_:` no trailing space when nodes empty); `test_unique_senders` kept verbatim because Agda `deriveNodesIfEmpty` now covers BU_ derivation uniformly.  **Architectural patterns established at E.10** (worth flagging for E.11/E.12/future cross-binding work): (a) **Push behavior into the FFI primitive, not into per-binding convenience helpers** (NEW lesson, captured as paragraph extension to `feedback_cross_language_parity.md`) тАФ the first attempt added a Python-only `_ensure_nodes_from_senders` shim above the FFI; user pushed back ("feels like 'you want to write in C++, but run this bit in Python'") so derivation was pushed into the Agda handler; convenience helpers above the FFI primitive create silent parity flaws when comparing equivalent operations across bindings.  (b) **Serializer/parser pairs must be inverse char-by-char** (NEW, saved as `feedback_serializer_parser_inverse.md`) тАФ a doc comment saying "we don't put quotes in our strings" is a precondition that fails the day a downstream feature carries user content through that string field.  (c) **State-non-mutating commands mirror `parseDBCText`'s shape** (reuse) тАФ return `(state , response)` without reading or writing state; avoids touching `StreamState` types and the proof obligations they carry.  **Cross-binding parity audit** before declaring done (advisor 2026-05-08): explicit `nodes` dedup symmetry confirmed (C++/Go/Agda all pass through non-empty lists; only `nubIds` runs on the empty branch); nested NotRequired list fields confirmed absent (every Tier-2 record's nested `signals`/`entries` lists are TypedDict-Required, no asymmetry to fix).  **Module count: 243 тЖТ 244** (+1 NEW, `--safe --without-K`); breakdown: **239** `--safe --without-K` + **4** `--safe --without-K --no-main` + **1** allowlisted `--without-K`-only Substrate.Unsafe.  **Gates passed at E.10 closure**: `cabal run shake -- build` 1m57s; `check-properties` 8m11s ("All proof modules type-checked successfully!"); `check-invariants` clean; `check-no-properties-in-runtime` clean; `check-erasure` 1m43s; `check-fidelity` 1m45s (1/1 test suites); `check-ffi-exports` clean (FFI surface unchanged at 11 entries тАФ routed via existing `processJSONLine`); `count-modules` 244; Python `pytest tests/` 751p+1s in 2.18s; Go `go test ./aletheia/ -count=1 -race` 3.057s; C++ `ctest --test-dir cpp/build` 8/8 in 22.43s; `pylint aletheia/` 10.00/10; `basedpyright aletheia/` 0/0/0; `gofmt -l . && go vet ./...` clean; `clang-format --dry-run --Werror` clean; clang-tidy clean rebuild with `-DALETHEIA_CLANG_TIDY=ON` clean.  **NO COMMIT** at user direction; UPD doc-state sync only. Supersedes 4c-(a) checkpoint shipped 2026-05-01 commit `cf091d8` on branch `b3d-3d5-format-dsl`** тАФ parseTopStmt restructured from 10-way `<|>` chain to 7-bucket head-character pattern dispatch (V / BA / BO / SI / SG / EV / CM); five simple section dispatchers (TVT / TM / TSG / TEV / TCM) and one generic `parseTopStmt-on-BA-head` attribute helper landed under `Properties/Aggregator/Dispatcher/`.  **Why the pivot (option A from a 3-option surfacing тАФ A reroute parseTopStmt; B head-class one-shot lemmas; C status quo)**: per-dispatcher elaboration of the 10-way chain at concrete-prefix input cost **15.7 GB residency / 273s** on a single dispatcher (TVT pilot under 10-way variant; localized via the type-only stub at 448 MB / 12s), with forward projection across 5 simples + ~33 TAT sub-cases тЙИ 3 hours wall + per-module residency at the `-M16G` tripwire тАФ not viable.  Head-dispatch reduces in 1 pattern-match step, then closes via 1- or 2-way `<|>`.  **Empirical wins** (each with `-N32 -M16G -s` after cache wipe): TVT 15.7 GB / 273s тЖТ **443 MB / 14s** (35├Ч memory, 19├Ч speedup); TM 570 MB / 9s; TSG 449 MB / 8s; TEV 476 MB / 8s; TCM 1.4 GB / 33s (5-target case-split on c.target because `emitComment-chars`'s `body` helper dispatches on target тАФ Agda only reduces the prefix once target is matched); generic Attribute helper 451 MB / 8s.  All under `-M16G` budget.  **What semantically changed**: zero behavioral drift тАФ the new parseTopStmt is **definitionally** equivalent to the old chain on every concrete input (cross-class head-disjointness already proven; same-bucket order preserved within each `<|>`).  All 760 Python tests pass including `test_format_dbc_round_trip` which exercises the DBC text parser/formatter roundtrip end-to-end through the FFI; full Shake build 1m50s; agda Main.agda exit 0.  **What landed in the commit** (11 files, +1159 -14): `TopLevel.agda` parseTopStmt rewrite (~70 LOC); 5 new simple dispatchers in `Properties/Aggregator/Dispatcher/Simple/{ValueTable,Message,SignalGroup,EnvVar,Comment}.agda` + `Simple.agda` fa├зade; new `Properties/Aggregator/Dispatcher/Attribute.agda` (generic `parseTopStmt-on-BA-head` lifts any of the 31 `parseAttrLine-roundtrip-*` slims into a parseTopStmt success in 1 line); previously WIP-uncommitted `Properties/Aggregator/Foundations.agda` + `BodyBridge.agda` + `ManyRoundtrip.agda` extension (`many-╬╖-roundtrip-with-lift`) committed alongside since they all type-check against the new dispatchers.  **What was deleted** (chain-era proofs obsolete under head-dispatch): `Properties/Aggregator/Dispatcher/AltChain.agda` (~280 LOC, 6 lift-altK helpers for the 10-way chain) + `HeadFails.agda` (~250 LOC, 27 leading-fail lemmas тАФ head-dispatch makes them automatic).  **Module count 209 тЖТ 218** (+9: 6 dispatcher modules + 1 fa├зade + Foundations + BodyBridge; Prior 2026-05-01 baseline: **Layer 4c WIP 2026-05-01 on branch `b3d-3d5-format-dsl`** тАФ universal target REFINED to `тИА d тЖТ WellFormedDBC d тЖТ parseText (formatText d) тЙб injтВВ d` per user-locked option (a). Decomposes via 5 applications of `foldr-emit-app` (foldr distributes over `++`) + 6 per-section `emit-map-T*-eq` bridges.  Attribute case requires `defs тЙб collectDefs attrs` (top-level invariant тАФ `defs` argument matches the `let defs = collectDefs attrs in foldr ...` baked into `emitAttributes-chars`).  All three type-check at `agda +RTS -N32 -M16G -RTS`.  **Architecture decided тАФ option ╬▒ (typed shadow + lift)** over option ╬▓ (per-section composition with 6 list-level lifts at parseTopStmt level тАФ re-derives 4b helper) and option ╬│ (lift-aware extension only).  **Remaining Layer 4c work**: (a) parseTopStmt dispatcher correctness (heaviest step) тАФ per-section `parseTopStmt-on-emitX defs pos x outer Stop ss-NL тЙб just (mkResult (liftTopStmt defs (TX x)) ... outer)` for X тИИ {ValueTable, Message, EnvVar, Comment, Attribute, SignalGroup}; 5 simple sections (~80-120 LOC each) compose existing slim roundtrips with parseTopStmt's 10-way alt-chain (mirror `Properties/Attributes/Line.agda`'s `parseAttrLine-lift-altK` helpers); attribute case (~600-1500 LOC) dispatches on `(DBCAttrDef ├Ч scope, DBCAttrDefault ├Ч AVxxx, DBCAttrAssign ├Ч target ├Ч AVxxx)` and routes through one of the existing 31 `parseAttrLine-roundtrip-*` slims with appropriate typedтЖТraw byte bridges. The smaller combined figure than 3c-A's 56% reflects 3c-B's per-shape ├Ч per-target dispatcher structure (5 std targets ├Ч 3 emit shapes + 2 rel targets ├Ч 3 emit shapes = 21 dispatchers, each ~30L); 3c-A's 56% came from a structural 5├Ч5 тЖТ 5-case collapse, 3c-B has no analogous collapse.  **Critical proof-engineering finding (validated 2026-05-01, see `feedback_with_abstraction_traps.md` + `feedback_emitsok_inj2_deep_pattern.md`)**: per-shape numeric dispatchers (RavDecRatFrac/-BareInt) initially used `with showXxx-chars-head-classify d` to extract head witnesses from a wide тИГтВВ ├Ч _тКО_ ╬г-type.  This OOM'd at -M16G after 6+ minutes for any target with the value at an injтВВ-deep altSum position.  Hoisting per-arm where-blocks to module-level helpers did NOT fix it.  Fix: replace `with` with **constructor pattern-matching** on the input (DecRat or тДд) + `projтВБ`/`projтВВ` projections to extract the head witness without `with`.  Pattern applied across 12 dispatcher clauses; compile-time dropped from 6+ min OOM to 13s.  User reinforced "with-abstraction often leads to a huge memory consumption ... you like using 'with' too much" тАФ promoted to behavioral note in `feedback_with_abstraction_traps.md` (default to projections / constructor pattern-match / helpers, `with` is last-resort). Prior 2026-04-29 baseline: Track B.3.d Layer 3 3d.5.d 3a Preamble DSL migration тЬЕ shipped 2026-04-29 commit `c5b34fb` тАФ production migration of all three preamble constructs (VERSION / BS_ / NS_) onto Format DSL under one PR via ╬╖-style wrap: `parseVersion = parse versionFmt >>= many parseNewline >>= pure`, `parseBitTiming = parse bitTimingFmt >>= many parseNewline >>= pure tt`, `parseNamespace = parse nsFmt >>= pure tt` (NS_'s body Format already captures the trailing blank line via discard-iso over `many nsLineFmt`).  New module `Format/Preamble.agda` (~670 file-LOC, **418 strict-LOC**) houses the three formats + universal `parseVersion-format-roundtrip` / `parseBitTiming-format-roundtrip` / `parseNamespace-format-roundtrip` lemmas + bridges (`emit-versionFmt-eq-emitVersion-chars-prefix` / `emit-bitTimingFmt-eq-emitBitTiming-chars-prefix` / `emit-nsFmt-eq-emitNamespace-chars`).  NS_ uses the **discard-iso pattern** over `many nsLineFmt`: inner pair tower's underlying carrier is `тКд ├Ч List NSLineShape`, the iso projects to `тКд` for the user-facing API while emitting the canonical 26-element body (25 specific keyword identifiers + 1 trailing blank line).  `NSLineShape = ns-blank | ns-keyword Identifier`; one body line dispatches via `altSum` over `blankLineFmt` (just `newlineFmt`) / `keywordLineFmt` (`'\t' + ident + wsOpt + newline`).  Termination certificate `parse-nsLineFmt-fail-on-stop` supplied for the `[]-fails` constructor of `EmitsOKMany` тАФ closes by char-class disjointness on the head of an `isNSLineStart c = isHSpace c тИи isNewlineStart c`-stopped suffix.  The 25 canonical keyword IDs are constructed via `mkKwId : (kw : String) тЖТ {valid : T (validIdentifierс╡З (toList kw))} тЖТ Identifier` using the load-bearing reduction canary from pre-3d.5.d's `_Scratch.agda` (typechecks iff `validIdentifierс╡З` reduces to `true` on closed keyword strings).  **Format DSL extensions**: (a) `wsCanonTab` тАФ canonical tab emit (`'\t' тИ╖ []`), parser one-or-more isHSpace; mirror of `ws` for tab-indented lines; used by NS_ keyword-line indent.  (b) `nonNewlineRun` тАФ empty canonical emit (`[]`), parser zero-or-more non-newline; used by BS_ opaque-tail consumer (formatter writes `BS_:\n\n`; parser consumes any non-newline tail before the LF).  **Spec preservation via `withWSCanonOne` (advisor-caught spec drift, fixed pre-commit)**: the NS_ header `:` separator slot uses the new sugar combinator `withWSCanonOne` (parser zero-or-more, canonical single space) тАФ matching the OLD `parseNamespace` accepting `"NS_:..."` (no whitespace required).  An initial `withWS` (one-or-more, mandatory) draft was caught by the advisor as a silent spec narrowing тАФ `nsFmt` would have rejected `"NS_:..."` while old code accepted it.  Type-equivalent fix (both EmitsOK obligations are `SuffixStops isHSpace`; both bridges close by `refl`).  Lesson captured in `feedback_format_dsl_ws_family_discipline.md`: when migrating a parser to Format DSL, audit each whitespace slot for permissiveness тАФ the four `withWS*` family members (`withWS`/`withWSOpt`/`withWSCanonOne`/`withWSCanonTab`) have distinct parser semantics that silently change parser permissiveness (bridge proofs only catch emit shape, not parse acceptance).  **Migrated modules**: `Properties/Preamble/Version.agda` 166 тЖТ 79 strict-LOC = 52% reduction; `Properties/Preamble/BitTiming.agda` 161 тЖТ 80 strict-LOC = 50%; `Properties/Preamble/Namespace.agda` 570 тЖТ 52 strict-LOC = **91%** reduction (heaviest 3a, was hand-written 864-file-LOC bind-chain through 25-keyword inductive `manyHelper-parseNSLine-body` + per-branch `parseNSLine-blank` / `parseNSLine-keyword` lemmas + length bounds).  Combined: 897 тЖТ 211 strict-LOC = **76% production-side reduction**.  Helpers added: `Lexer.isNonNewline : Char тЖТ Bool`, `Primitives.parseWS-one-tab`, `Primitives.map-nothing` (`_<$>_` analogue of `bind-nothing`).  **Where-clause vs module-level helpers (load-bearing)**: initial draft had `nsLineFmt`'s iso forward/backward functions as where-bound; under elaboration these did NOT reduce definitionally at consumer call sites, blocking `EmitsOK-keyword-line` (the goal stayed `Identifier.name kw != Identifier.name kw ++ emit (withWSOpt newlineFmt) tt`).  Fix: hoist `ns-line-fwd` / `ns-line-bwd` / `ns-line-inv` to module-level `private` definitions.  Same fix applied to `versionFmt` and `keywordLineFmt`'s pair-projection helpers (replaced with inline `projтВБ` / `projтВВ` lambdas).  **EmitsOK shape mismatch via `++`-association**: `emit (withWSOpt newlineFmt) tt` stays abstract under Agda elaboration, so the goal `(Identifier.name kw ++ emit (withWSOpt newlineFmt) tt) ++ rest` doesn't reduce against a precondition of shape `SuffixStops isHSpace (Identifier.name kw ++ '\n' тИ╖ rest)`.  Fix: change precondition shape to `SuffixStops isHSpace ((Identifier.name kw ++ '\n' тИ╖ []) ++ rest)` in three places тАФ generalises to any future migration where a Format leaf has an abstract emit that needs to bridge a precondition. ## Project Phases

### Phase 1: Core Infrastructure тЬЕ COMPLETE

**Scope**: Build the foundational formally verified components

**Delivered**:
- Parser combinators with structural recursion
- CAN signal encoding/decoding (8-byte frames, 11-bit IDs)
- DBC parser (JSON format)
- Build pipeline (Agda тЖТ Haskell тЖТ Python)
- Basic protocol integration (Echo, ParseDBC, ExtractSignal, InjectSignal)
- Python wrapper

**Status**: 100% Complete

---

### Phase 2A: LTL Core + Real-World Support тЬЕ COMPLETE

**Scope**: Add Linear Temporal Logic verification and extended CAN support

**Delivered**:
- LTL syntax (Always, Eventually, Until, Next, And, Or, Not, Atomic)
- Coinductive and bounded trace semantics
- Signal predicates (Equals, LessThan, GreaterThan, LessThanOrEqual, GreaterThanOrEqual, Between, ChangedBy, StableWithin)
- Model checker with decidable comparisons
- Extended 29-bit CAN ID support
- Signal multiplexing (Always | When conditions)
- Python LTL DSL

**Status**: 100% Complete

---

### Phase 2B: Streaming Architecture тЬЕ COMPLETE

**Scope**: Streaming protocol with O(1) memory and production-ready Python API

**Delivered**:

**Phase 2B.1 - Core Protocol**:
- JSON streaming protocol (request-response via FFI)
- Message router (command/data routing)
- Command handlers (parseDBC, setProperties, startStream, endStream)
- StreamState validation
- Haskell I/O shim
- Python AletheiaClient (FFI via ctypes)

**Phase 2B.2 - Streaming LTL**:
- Incremental LTL evaluation (O(1) memory)
- Coinductive streaming interface
- Frame modification mid-stream
- Throughput: 9,229 fps (108 us/frame via FFI; improved to 9,704 fps after Ro╚Щu simplification тАФ the bottom-up LTLf simplification rules from Ro╚Щu's runtime verification work). C++, JSON path, single-threaded, Ryzen 9 5950X baseline

**Phase 2B.3 - Polish**:
- Counterexample generation with violation details
- Rich error messages
- Python DSL refinement
- Performance tuning (parallel GHC)
- Comprehensive documentation

**Extension - Signal Operations**:
- AletheiaClient: Unified client with streaming + signal operations
- Build/update CAN frames with multiple signals
- Extract all signals with partitioned results
- Rich result objects (values/errors/absent signals)

**Status**: 100% Complete

---

### Phase 3: Verification + Performance тЬЕ COMPLETE

**Scope**: Formal correctness proofs and performance optimization

**Goals** (6 total):
1. тЬЕ Parser soundness proofs - COMPLETE
   - `Parser/Properties.agda`: 30 proven properties (monad laws, position tracking, parse determinism)
   - `Protocol/JSON/Properties.agda`: 12 proven properties (schema soundness, lookup correctness)
2. тЬЕ LTL semantics correctness proofs - COMPLETE
   - `LTL/Adequacy.agda`: Adequacy theorem proving `stepL` correct against denotational LTLf semantics
   - All 13 operators proven sound (four-layer proof structure, 1,061 lines)
   - `LTL/Semantics.agda`: Denotational LTLf semantics (`тЯж_тЯз`)
   - No postulates, pure coalgebraic reasoning
3. тЬЕ CAN encoding correctness proofs - COMPLETE
   - `Data/BitVec/Conversion.agda`: bitVec-roundtrip and bitVecToтДХ-bounded (no postulates!)
   - `CAN/Endianness.agda`: extractBits-injectBits-roundtrip, injectBits-preserves-disjoint, injectBits-commute
   - `CAN/Encoding.agda`: injectSignal-preserves-disjoint-bits (key structural lemma)
   - `CAN/Batch/Properties.agda`: injectAll-preserves-disjoint (batch operations preserve extraction)
   - Mixed byte-order injection commutativity proven in Phase 5
4. тЬЕ DSL translation correctness proofs - COMPLETE
   - `LTL/JSON/Format.agda`: formatSignalPredicate, formatLTL, ltlDepth functions
   - `LTL/JSON/Properties.agda`: Roundtrip and completeness proofs
   - Proven: parseLTL (ltlDepth ╧Ж) (formatLTL ╧Ж) тЙб just ╧Ж
5. тЬЕ Three-valued signal semantics - COMPLETE
   - `LTL/SignalPredicate.agda`: TruthVal (True/False/Unknown/Pending), Kleene logic, SignalCache
   - `LTL/Incremental.agda`: Inconclusive state, safety vs liveness semantics
   - `LTL/Coalgebra.agda`: Mirrored Inconclusive handling for adequacy proof
   - Key improvement: No frame filtering needed - Unknown signals continue monitoring
6. тЬЕ Performance optimization - COMPLETE
   - Target: 8,000 fps (125 us/frame for 1 Mbps CAN bus)
   - Achieved: 9,704 fps (103 us/frame, C++ single-threaded JSON path, CAN 2.0B Stream LTL with 2 properties, Ryzen 9 5950X, 10k frames ├Ч 5 runs) тАФ 3.03x speedup (initially 9,229 fps; improved after Ro╚Щu simplification)
   - Steps: GHC compiler flags, FinтЖТтДХ elimination, FFI shared library (eliminated IPC)

**Status**: Complete (started 2025-12-17)
**Completion**: 100% (6/6 goals complete)

---

### Phase 4: Production Hardening тЬЕ COMPLETE

**Scope**: Make Aletheia usable by non-developers and production-ready for deployment

**Design principle**: Four tiers of user interface, all compiling to the same
verified core:

| Tier | User | Interface |
|------|------|-----------|
| Excel | Technician | Fill in numbers in spreadsheet templates, press Run |
| YAML | Test engineer | Edit declarative config files (version-controllable, CI/CD) |
| Check API | Scripter | `Check.signal("Speed").never_exceeds(220)` |
| DSL | Developer | `Signal("Speed").less_than(220).always()` (full LTL) |

**Goals** (11 total):

1. тЬЕ Check API тАФ high-level property library (`python/aletheia/checks.py`) тАФ COMPLETE
   - 6 simple conditions: `never_exceeds`, `never_below`, `stays_between`, `never_equals`, `equals`, `settles_between`
   - 3 when/then trigger/response patterns with `.within(ms)` deadline
   - Fluent API: `Check.signal("Speed").never_exceeds(220)` returns `CheckResult`
   - Metadata: `.named()` and `.severity()` chainable setters
   - Industry vocabulary: no LTL knowledge required

2. тЬЕ YAML loader (`python/aletheia/yaml_loader.py`) тАФ COMPLETE
   - Declarative check definitions in YAML files
   - Schema: signal + condition + value/min/max + within_ms + severity
   - Supports simple checks and when/then response-time checks
   - `load_checks()` accepts file path or inline YAML string
   - Clear error messages referencing check names

3. тЬЕ Excel loader (`python/aletheia/excel_loader.py`) тАФ COMPLETE
   - `load_dbc_from_excel()`: DBC definitions from spreadsheet (hex/decimal message IDs, multiplexed signals)
   - `load_checks_from_excel()`: Simple checks + when/then checks from two sheets
   - `create_template()`: Generates blank .xlsx with bold headers and three sheets (DBC, Checks, When-Then)
   - Row-level error messages, openpyxl type stubs for strict type checking
   - Dependency: `openpyxl>=3.1` (added to pyproject.toml)

4. тЬЕ CLI tool (`python -m aletheia`) тАФ COMPLETE
   - `aletheia check` тАФ run checks from YAML/Excel against a CAN log file
   - `aletheia extract` тАФ extract signals from a single frame
   - `aletheia signals` тАФ list signals in a DBC (or Excel)
   - `aletheia validate` тАФ validate DBC for structural issues
   - Exit codes: 0=pass, 1=violations, 2=error; `--json` flag for structured output
   - 41 tests (pure-Python + FFI integration)

5. тЬЕ CAN log reader (`python/aletheia/can_log.py`) тАФ COMPLETE
   - `load_can_log()` (eager) and `iter_can_log()` (lazy iterator) via `python-can`
   - Supports ASC, BLF, CSV, SQLite .db, candump .log, MF4, TRC with auto-detection
   - Returns `CANFrameTuple` 7-NamedTuple (timestamp, can_id, dlc, data, extended, brs, esi) тАФ feeds directly to `send_frame()`
   - Full public API migrated from `list[int]` to `bytearray`
   - DLC-aware normalization: pads/truncates data to DLC byte count
   - Options: `skip_error_frames`, `skip_remote_frames`, `on_error`

6. тЬЕ Richer violation diagnostics тАФ COMPLETE
   - `CheckResult` carries `signal_name` and `condition_desc` from all builders
   - `AletheiaClient.send_frame()` auto-enriches violations: extracts signal value, builds human-readable reason
   - Bounded extraction cache (256 unique frames) keeps throughput above 8,000 fps target
   - `PropertyViolationResponse` extended with `signal_name`, `actual_value`, `condition` fields
   - CLI and all consumers get enriched violations for free via client-level enrichment

7. тЬЕ Deployment guide + install/uninstall тАФ COMPLETE (Shakefile, `cabal run shake -- install`)

8. тЬЕ Tutorial / cookbook тАФ COMPLETE (`docs/guides/TUTORIAL.md`, `docs/guides/COOKBOOK.md`, `docs/guides/QUICKSTART.md`)

9. тЬЕ DBC Validator тАФ COMPLETE
   - Agda: `DBC/Validator.agda` (new), `DBC/Types.agda`, `Protocol/Message.agda`, `Protocol/Routing.agda`, `Protocol/StreamState.agda`
   - `validateDBCFull : DBC тЖТ List ValidationIssue` тАФ 16 checks (8 error, 8 warning), all issues accumulated
   - `IssueCode` enum: 15 codes covering structural, physical, and authoring issues
   - Decidable types throughout (`_тЙЯ-CANId_`, `any?`, `_тИИ?_`, `signalPairValid?`)
   - Dual-layer validation: `parseDBC` runs both `validateDBC` + `validateDBCFull`
   - **Formally verified**: soundness + completeness proof (1,267 lines, 6 modules)
   - Python: `client.validate_dbc()`, `cli validate` subcommand
   - All tests pass, 0 regressions

10. тЬЕ Signal staleness bug demo тАФ COMPLETE
    - Engine ECU freeze scenario: FrameCounter counter frozen
    - Demo files: `engine_ecu_sim.py`, `test_engine_naive.py`, `demo_ltl_bug.py`
    - 8 naive unit tests that pass against buggy ECU тЬУ
    - Aletheia LTL catches 34 frozen alive counter violations тЬУ

11. тЬЕ Default properties + `add_checks()` API тАФ COMPLETE
    - `AletheiaClient(default_checks=[...])` constructor param
    - `add_checks()` merges defaults + session checks atomically
    - `--defaults` CLI argument wired in `_cmd_check()` via `_load_defaults()`
    - `_run_checks()` accepts `default_checks` param, uses `add_checks()`
    - 9 FFI integration tests in `test_default_checks.py`, all pass

**End-of-stream property finalization** тЬЕ COMPLETE
- Added Bool resolved flag to safety operators (Always, Release, MetricAlways, MetricRelease)
- `finalizeEval : LTLEvalState тЖТ FinalVerdict` determines Holds/Fails at end-of-stream
- `handleEndStream-State` calls `finalizeEval` on each property
- `Response.Complete` now carries `List PropertyResult` with per-property verdicts
- 7 integration tests verify all finalization behaviors
- Renamed `ThreeVal` тЖТ `TruthVal` (now 4 constructors: True, False, Unknown, Pending)

**Documentation**: Interface Guide (`docs/reference/INTERFACES.md`) with Check API, YAML, and Excel
end-to-end workflows. Cross-linked from README, INDEX, and Python API Guide.

**Demos**: 11 demo scripts + data files in `examples/demo/` (see [Documentation Index](docs/INDEX.md#examples) for full listing)

**Presentation**: `docs/presentation/index.html` тАФ 36-slide reveal.js deck for product council (1 hour + Q&A)

**Status**: Complete (2026-02-06 to 2026-02-22)
**Completion**: 100% (11/11 goals complete)

---

### Phase 5: Optional Extensions тЬЕ COMPLETE

**Scope**: Features driven by user feedback and real-world needs

**Delivered**:
- тЬЕ DBC pretty-printer with formatтЖТparse roundtrip proofs (7 commits, +1,834/-393 lines)
- тЬЕ Encode/decode batch roundtrip proofs: `injectAll-roundtrip` proves that after `injectAll`, extracting any injected signal returns its value. Bridge lemmas (`roundtrip-unsignedтЖТIR`, `roundtrip-signedтЖТIR`) connect single-signal roundtrips to the batch predicate. Dead commutativity proofs (~200 lines) removed from `Encoding/Properties.agda`.
- тЬЕ Decidable precondition helpers for capstone theorem: decidable equality chain (`_тЙЯ-SignalPresence_`, `_тЙЯ-SignalDef_`, `_тЙЯ-DBCSignal_` in `DBC/Properties.agda`) and decidable checkers (`allAlwaysPresent?`, `allFromMessage?`, `pairsDistinct?` in `CAN/Batch/Properties.agda`). Users can now compute the 3 structural preconditions of `validDBC-roundtrip` automatically.
- тЬЕ Decidable value representability: `Representable` predicate with decidable checker `representable?` and bridge lemma `allRepresentableтЖТallRoundtrip` (~120 lines in `CAN/Batch/Properties.agda`). Decides whether each (signal, value) pair is exactly representable, then derives `AllRoundtrip` from `ValidDBC`. Last non-decidable capstone precondition now decidable.
- тЬЕ extractAllSignals completeness proof: `extractAll-complete` proves `totalEntries (extractAllSignalsFromMessage dbc frame msg) тЙб length (DBCMessage.signals msg)` (~40 lines in `CAN/Batch/Properties.agda`). Every signal produces exactly one entry across the three result partitions (values, errors, absent). Proof by foldr induction with `with`-decomposition of the recursive accumulator.
- тЬЕ Mixed byte-order injection commutativity: `injectPayload-commute-mixed` proves disjoint `injectPayload` calls commute for all 4 byte-order combinations (~278 lines in `CAN/Endianness.agda`). 4-layer proof: swap-conjugation converts cross-BO operations to `applyWrites` at physical positions, then existing `applyWrites-comm` handles commutativity. Layered architecture: concrete Vec Byte 8 тЖТ single BitWrite тЖТ write list тЖТ AllDiffPos structural conversion тЖТ 4-case dispatch.

- тЬЕ C++23 binding (`cpp/`): Complete client library wrapping `libaletheia-ffi.so` via `dlopen`. Strong types (`std::byte` frame data, validated newtypes for CAN ID / DLC / BitPosition / etc., `Rational` for exact signal values), `std::expected` for errors, RAII state lifecycle, dependency injection via `IBackend` interface. Mock backend for testing without Agda core. Hash-map `DbcIndex` for O(1) signal lookups. Formula depth limit (100). 158 unit + 34 integration + 33 YAML + 47 Excel TEST_CASEs (272 total) across 4 runtime test suites + static_asserts in a 5th compile-time suite, `ctest 5/5` PASS (see Key Metrics). 11+ rounds of code review тАФ all categories pass, clang-format and clang-tidy enforced as hard gates (zero violations/warnings). CMake build with `FetchContent` (nlohmann/json, Catch2), `SOVERSION`, install/export for `find_package()`.

- тЬЕ Go binding (`go/`): Complete client library wrapping `libaletheia-ffi.so` via cgo + dlopen. Strong types (`[]byte` payload with DLC-based validation, sealed interfaces for CanID/Predicate/Formula/SignalPresence/FrameResponse, validated newtypes for CAN ID / DLC, `Rational` for exact signal values). `Backend` interface abstracts FFI; `MockBackend` for testing, `FFIBackend` for production. Goroutine-safe `Client` (`sync.Mutex`), double-close safe (`sync.Once`), GHC RTS init thread-pinned. `slog` structured logging (12 event types, `ClientOption`/`WithLogger`). Hash-map indexes in `Dbc` for O(1) signal lookups. Formula depth limit (100). 16 source files + 14 test files in `go/aletheia/` (218 tests), plus a separate `go/excel/` module (58 tests) тАФ all pass with `-race`. 23 rounds of code review (AGENTS.md). `ffi_nocgo.go` build tag fallback for non-cgo builds.

- тЬЕ C header (`include/aletheia.h`): Documents the 5 C-callable FFI functions + GHC RTS initialization contract. The contract all language bindings implement against. Shakefile packaging target (`cabal run shake -- dist`) bundles .so + header.

- тЬЕ Big-endian (Motorola) signal fix: `convertStartBit` at parse time (`DBC/JSONParser.agda`), `unconvertStartBit` at format time (`DBC/Formatter.agda`). Byte-order-aware `BitsInFrame` predicate and `checkSignalExceedsDLC` validator. All soundness/completeness proofs updated (`ErrorChecks.agda`, `Composition.agda`). Verified against cantools for 5 signal types (byte-aligned, non-byte-aligned, single-bit, cross-byte, full-frame). Example DBC updated with BE signals.

- тЬЕ Violation enrichment (all bindings): Client-side enrichment pipeline тАФ formula description, signal value extraction with bounded cache, human-readable violation reason. Implemented in Python (`_client.py`), C++ (`enrich.hpp`/`enrich.cpp`), and Go (`enrich.go`). 235-line Python enrichment test suite. Type audit across all bindings (removed redundant optionals where types have natural empty states).

- тЬЕ Docker images: `Dockerfile` (multi-stage from-source build) and `Dockerfile.runtime` (lightweight from pre-built dist). Runtime image is ~200 MB (python:3.13-slim + .so bundle + pip deps). `ALETHEIA_LIB` env var for library discovery. `shake docker` target builds the runtime image. Fat single-file .so investigated and deferred тАФ GHC's static archives lack `-fPIC`, so self-contained `.so` would require rebuilding GHC. Current approach: 15 `.so` files with `RPATH=$ORIGIN` (9.6 MB compressed tarball).

- тЬЕ Cross-language benchmark suite (2026-03-26): Throughput, latency, and scaling benchmarks for all three language bindings with machine-readable JSON output. Runner script (`benchmarks/run_all.sh`), comparison script (`benchmarks/compare.py`). DLC serialization bug fixed in Go/C++ (was sending DLC code instead of byte count in DBC serialization). Hot-path optimizations: ack fast path (byte-level response check) and direct string serialization (bypass nlohmann/json.Marshal for frame commands) in C++ and Go.

- тЬЕ Binary FFI for streaming hot path (2026-03-27): `aletheia_send_frame` binary entry point eliminates JSON serialization for CAN data frames. Haskell shim constructs MAlonzo types (`Vec Byte n`, `TimedFrame`, `CANFrame`) directly from raw bytes. `processFrameDirect` in Main.agda calls `handleDataFrame` directly. All 67 modules use `--safe`. Agda proofs in `Protocol/FrameProcessor/Properties.agda`: 15 properties covering state machine guards, streaming decomposition, ack/violation soundness + completeness, predicate table faithfulness, and signal cache correctness. All three bindings updated with strong types at API surface (`Timestamp`/`CanId`/`Dlc` тАФ raw C types only inside FFI implementation). CMakeLists.txt fixed to default to Release build. Result: **4.3x CAN 2.0B** (11kтЖТ48k fps), **9.1x CAN-FD** (1.9kтЖТ17k fps).

- тЬЕ Dead code removal + proof completion (2026-03-27): Removed vestigial JSON data frame path (`parseDataFrame`, `Request` type, `DataFrame`, `processStream`, `parseRequest-sound` proof) тАФ all bindings use binary FFI exclusively. Main.agda upgraded from `--sized-types` to `--safe`. New proofs: `initProc-correct` (initial LTL state correctness, `LTL/Coalgebra/Properties.agda`), response formatting correctness (8 refl proofs, `Protocol/ResponseFormat/Properties.agda`). All provable items in the proof assessment are now proven; only the MAlonzo FFI trust boundary remains (outside Agda's type system, mitigated by build-time checks and smoke tests).

- тЬЕ CAN-FD support (started 2026-03-23, completed 2026-03-25): Variable-length payloads up to 64 bytes, DLC 0-15 with non-linear mapping (see [PROTOCOL.md](docs/architecture/PROTOCOL.md#1-parsedbc) for details). 13-step plan + 7 review fixes fully executed:
  - Steps 1-4: Agda core types (`CANFrame n`, `TimedFrame` dependent record, protocol messages generic, `physicalBitPos` parameterized, validation layer updated)

  - Review fixes (F1-F7): Stale comments fixed, `TimedFrame.dlcValid` invariant added, DLC bounds check (`тЙд 15`) at protocol entry points, `ValidDLC` tightened to exact CAN/CAN-FD byte counts via `bytesToDlc`, `buildFrame` parameterized by DLC, `PhysicallyDisjoint` parameterized by frame byte count, disjointness proofs generalized (`lookupSafe-swapBytes`, `swap-updateSafe-swap` from case-enumeration to induction, `injectSignal-preserves-disjoint-bits-physical` from `CANFrame 8` to `тИА {n}`, capstone `validDBC-roundtrip` uses message DLC directly)
  - Code review round (R1-R5): `WellFormed.agda` uses `max-physical-bits` constant (was hardcoded 512), accurate CAN-FD comments in `Endianness.agda`, explicit `payloadSize = dlcToBytes dlc` in `Routing.agda`, numeric conversions extracted to `Encoding/Arithmetic.agda` (Encoding.agda 391тЖТ336 lines), `readBit-updateSafe-same`/`readBit-updateSafe-diff` proof helpers in `Endianness/Properties.agda`

- тЬЕ Pipeline soundness fix (2026-03-28): Discovered 8 unsound absorption rules in `simplify/absorb` (Coalgebra.agda). Proofs complete: `absorb-runL`, `simplify-runL`, `pipeline-adequate`, `production-adequate` in `Adequacy/Pipeline.agda`.

- тЬЕ DeltaPredicate split (2026-04-02): `DeltaPredicate` now has two constructors: `ChangedBy` (directional тАФ sign of delta determines direction: positive `curr - prev тЙе delta`, negative `curr - prev тЙд delta`) and `StableWithin` (magnitude tolerance тАФ `|curr - prev| тЙд tolerance`). Previous `ChangedBy` semantics (`|curr - prev| тЙд delta`) were a confused mix. JSON protocol: `"changedBy"` predicate with `"delta"` field, new `"stableWithin"` predicate with `"tolerance"` field. Roundtrip proof updated (`refl`). All three bindings updated with `StableWithin` type + enrichment display. Python: `Signal.stable_within(tol)` method. C++: `StableWithin` struct + `Tolerance` newtype. Go: `StableWithin` struct + `Tolerance` type, negative delta now allowed in `ChangedBy`.

- тЬЕ AGENTS.md (2026-03-29, rewritten 2026-03-31): Review protocol document for all languages (Agda 16 categories, Go 22, C++ 22, Python, Documentation 19). Origin-blind finding rules: findings have no origin, age, or owner -- they are things that are wrong and get fixed. C++ section adds clang-format and clang-tidy as hard gates (zero violations/warnings required).

- тЬЕ RTS cores for all bindings (2026-03-31): GHC RTS `-N` flag configurable in all three language bindings. Python: `AletheiaClient(rts_cores=N)`. All: once-per-process, warn on mismatch, never reinitializable. Enables multi-bus monitoring with parallel GHC capabilities.

### Phase 5.1: Proof Gaps & Spec Observations тЬЕ COMPLETE

**Scope**: Address proof gaps and specification limitations identified during code review

- ~~Metric operator bounds unproven~~ тЬЕ PROVEN (2026-04-07): 13 properties in Coalgebra/Properties.agda тАФ stepL terminal at window expiry, runL immediate resolution, past-window monotonicity, remaining-time anti-monotonicity
- ~~Signal cache monotonicity/coherence unproven~~ тЬЕ PROVEN (2026-04-07): 10 properties across Cache/Properties.agda (6) + FrameProcessor/Properties.agda (4) тАФ entry preservation through updates/signal processing/frame processing, timestamp bound preservation (AllTimestampsтЙд), cache size non-decreasing
- ~~rangesOverlap incorrect at len=0 + dual overlap algorithms~~ тЬЕ RESOLVED (2026-04-07): removed rangesOverlap entirely; BatchFrameBuilding.signalsOverlap/anyOverlap/hasOverlaps now delegate to physicallyDisjoint? from DBC/Properties.agda (endianness-aware, formally proven)
- ~~Single-level multiplexing only~~ тЬЕ RESOLVED (2026-04-07): SignalPresence.When now takes ListтБ║ тДХ (multi-value mux). Supports extended DBC multiplexing (SG_MUL_VAL_). JSON field `multiplex_value` тЖТ `multiplex_values` (array). All Agda proofs (roundtrip, overlap, CanCoexist) updated. Python/C++/Go bindings updated.
- ~~Nested multiplexing~~ тЬЕ RESOLVED (2026-04-07): `checkSignalPresence` now recursively walks the multiplexor chain bottom-up via `walkMux` with fuel = `length signals` (max acyclic chain length). Cycle detection by fuel exhaustion тЖТ `MultiplexorCycle` IssueCode (replaces `MultiplexorNotAlwaysPresent`). 4 properties in `SignalExtraction/Properties.agda` via `checkPresenceP` helper. Cross-language tests: 5 Python (real FFI) + 5 C++ integration (real FFI) + 6 Go mock. Drive-by: 8 pre-existing basedpyright errors in `_client.py` fixed via `map(int, struct.unpack_from(...))` consolidation.
- ~~MetricEventually suc-encoded time~~ тЬЕ CLOSED (2026-04-07): non-issue. Suc-encoding is on `startTime` (not `window`); deadline 0 is representable and means "must hold now". Already documented in Syntax.agda lines 30-44.
- ~~BatchFrameBuilding name/index duplication~~ тЬЕ CLOSED (2026-04-07): already resolved. `LookupStrategy K` record + `lookupSignalsG`/`buildFrameG`/`updateFrameG` generics. The six named functions are one-liner aliases over shared implementations.
- ~~DBC roundtrip requires empty metadata (groups/envvars/vtables)~~ тЬЕ RESOLVED (2026-04-07): Added metadata parsers (parseSignalGroupList, parseEnvironmentVarList, parseValueTableList) to JSONParser.agda with parseOptionalArray for backward compatibility. MetadataRoundtrip.agda proves unconditional roundtrip for all three types. Removed empty-metadata preconditions from WellFormedDBCRT. Fixed pre-existing bug in MessageWF.agda (stale proof hidden by interface cache). 90 Agda modules.
- LTLf completeness and liveness proofs (see sub-items):
  - ~~Two-valued agreement (full completeness)~~ тЬЕ PROVEN (2026-04-07): Agreement.agda тАФ `runL table proc ╧Г тЙб тЯж denot table proc тЯз ╧Г` when all atomic predicates return True/False (TwoValued). Uses `rewrite` + identity lemmas (`тИзTV-true-l`, `тИиTV-false-l`, etc.) to handle overlapping `тИзTV`/`тИиTV` clause non-reduction. Four metric helpers extracted for termination. 91 Agda modules.
  - ~~Metric resolution guarantee~~ тЬЕ PROVEN (2026-04-07): Coalgebra/Properties.agda тАФ `runL-definite` (runL only ever True/False), `runL-monotonic-mtl-sound` (composes adequacy + mtl-equiv via Sound transport), `runL-monotonic-{False,True}` corollaries. On finite monotonic traces, definite тЯж_тЯзтВШ verdicts are mirrored exactly by runL тАФ no Unknown, no Continue.
  - ~~Finalization soundness~~ тЬЕ PROVEN (2026-04-07): Coalgebra/Properties.agda тАФ `finalize-empty-equiv : verdictToSV (finalizeL proc) тЙб тЯж denot table proc тЯз []`. Propositional equality between the operational end-of-stream verdict and the denotational empty-trace evaluation, proven by structural induction on all 13 LTL constructors. Connects operational "didn't find it" to denotational "it's not there." Closes the last LTLf liveness sub-item.
  - ~~Safety-liveness duality~~ тЬЕ PROVEN (2026-04-07): Semantics/Duality.agda тАФ `eventually-always-dual`, `always-eventually-dual`, `until-release-dual`, `release-until-dual`. Four pointwise identities on `тЯж_тЯз` proven by structural induction on ╧Г + de Morgan + double-negation lifted from Kleene logic. Added `notTV-involutive`, `deMorgan-тИз`, `deMorgan-тИи` to TruthVal/Properties.agda. 92 Agda modules.
- ~~No bound proof for indexHelper indices~~ тЬЕ PROVEN (2026-04-07): FrameProcessor/Properties.agda Property 27 тАФ `AllBelow : тДХ тЖТ LTL тДХ тЖТ Set` predicate, `indexHelper-bound`, `indexFormula-bound`, `simplify-bound`, `stepL-bound`, `lookupAtom-total`, `mkPredTable-bounded`. Layered proof: AllBelow weakening + indexHelper monotonicity + bound preservation through both `simplify` (via per-And/Or `absorb` helpers) and `stepL` (via `combineAnd`/`combineOr` lemmas through `ResultBound`). The `nothing тЖТ Unknown` branch in `mkPredTable` is now provably dead code; lookup is total over reachable indices.
- ~~Monotonic predicate defined but unused in Agda~~ тЬЕ RESOLVED (2026-04-07): `handleDataFrame` now enforces timestamp monotonicity directly in Agda via `checkMonotonic` тАФ backward frames (`timestamp tf < timestamp prev`) are rejected with a new `NonMonotonicTimestamp` `HandlerError` (code `handler_non_monotonic_timestamp`). The `prev` field in the `Streaming` constructor (previously set but never read) is now repurposed as the monotonicity anchor. 6 new properties in FrameProcessor/Properties.agda Property 28: `checkMonotonic-first`/`-тЙе`/`-<` (runtime check classification), `handleDataFrame-rejects-regress` (backward rejected, prev unchanged тАФ rejected frame never becomes new anchor), `handleDataFrame-accepts-monotonic` (тЙе anchor preserves iteration decomposition), `handleDataFrame-first-frame` (nothing prev always accepted). These bridge the streaming pipeline to the existing `Trace.CANTrace.Monotonic` predicate that Coalgebra metric LTL theorems take as hypothesis. Duplicated runtime checks removed from Python (`_client.py`), C++ (`client.cpp`/`client.hpp`), and Go (`client.go`) тАФ Agda is now single source of truth. New `HandlerNonMonotonicTimestamp` added to C++ `ErrorCode` enum and Go `CodeHandlerNonMonotonicTimestamp` constant (41 total error codes, was 40). Cross-binding tests: 1 Python real-FFI (`test_send_frame_non_monotonic_timestamp`), 1 C++ integration (`[integration][monotonic]`), 1 Go mock (`TestSendFrame_NonMonotonicTimestamp`). `Main/Binary.agda` "CALLER CONTRACT" comment replaced with pointer to the in-core enforcement.

**Post-implementation review round (2026-04-07)** тАФ 11 findings (C1/C2/C3 + H1тАУH6 + D1тАУD3 + X1/X2) closed after Phase 5.1 14/14 landed:

- **C1** Monotonic bridge lemma from `handleDataFrame` тЖТ trace-level `Trace.CANTrace.Monotonic` (closes the enforcement тЖФ theorem-hypothesis gap)
- **C2** `LTL/Adequacy/Agreement.agda` module-header sweep тАФ documents that `TwoValued` does NOT hold universally on `mkPredTable` (dead-code Unknown branch, Property 27); both `adequacy` (cold start) and `warm-cache-agreement` (steady state) are production-applicable, with the reasoning chain written out
- **C3** Warm-cache agreement chain: `evalPredicate-cache-definite` тЖТ `lookupAtom-warm` тЖТ `warm-cache-table-definite` тЖТ `warm-cache-bounded-twovalued` тЖТ `agreement-bounded` тЖТ `warm-cache-agreement`. Composes Property 27 with cache warmness to discharge `agreement`'s `TwoValued` precondition on steady-state hot paths
- **H1+H4** Chained `rewrite` blocks in SimplifySound + Agreement rewritten using identity lemmas from `TruthVal/Properties.agda` (unblocks overlapping Kleene clauses without with-abstraction memory blowup)
- **H2** Brittle `congтВВ f refl eq` in `runL-and-right-True` merged into single `congтВВ f A (trans B C)` to avoid unsolvable metavariable from non-injective `_тИзTV_`/`_тИиTV_`
- **H3** Two-sided `sound-transport : mтВБтЙбmтВВ тЖТ dтВБтЙбdтВВ тЖТ Sound mтВБ dтВБ тЖТ Sound mтВВ dтВВ` combinator extracted in `Adequacy.agda` (composed from existing `sound-transport-monitor`/`sound-transport-denot`); `runL-monotonic-False`/`runL-monotonic-True` now single-call
- **H5** Legacy `inspect` тЖТ modern `with expr in eq` migration in 3 files: `CAN/Encoding/Properties.agda` (2 uses), `Data/BitVec/Conversion.agda` (`parity-decomp`), `Protocol/JSON/Properties.agda` (`parseDBC-sound` nested match with 17+ absurdity clauses)
- **H6** Fuel justification documented for `walkMux` (`Validator/Checks.agda`) and `checkPresenceP` (`CAN/SignalExtraction.agda`) тАФ fuel тЙд length signals, strictly decreasing, pigeonhole soundness argument, validator check 5 (`MultiplexorCycle`) discharges cyclic inputs
- **D1+D2+D3** `buildResult`/`updateResult`/`formatResult` deduplicated in `Protocol/Handlers.agda` тЖТ single private `frameResponse : String тЖТ тИА {n} тЖТ FrameError тКО Vec Byte n тЖТ Response` helper; update handlers pre-apply `Data.Sum.mapтВВ CANFrame.payload`; all 4 where-block local helpers removed across `handleBuildFrame`, `handleBuildFrameByIndex`, `handleUpdateFrame`, `handleUpdateFrameByIndex`

- **X2** Agent D deferred non-blockers recorded in memory `project_system_review_deferred.md`: 10.1 Timestamp=тДХ unrefined (no unit phantom), 11.1 `mkPredTable` invariant runtime-not-type-level, 14.1 `Main.agda` re-exports implicit, 15.1/15.2 large Properties files (Encoding 1582 lines; FrameProcessor 28+ properties), 12 unproven proof-breadth gaps (`parseDBC-complete` + `formatDBC тИШ parseDBCWithErrors` roundtrip; walkMux/checkPresenceP propositional agreement; cache coherence `cache hit тЗТ verdict matches fresh extraction`)

**Timestamp dimensional refinement (2026-04-08)** тАФ Closes deferred non-blocker 10.1 from `project_system_review_deferred.md`. `TimedFrame.timestamp` and both `TraceEvent` error/remote timestamps now have type `Timestamp ╬╝s` (microseconds), a single-constructor record with an erased (`@0`) `TimeUnit` phantom parameter. New module `Aletheia.Trace.Time` (`src/Aletheia/Trace/Time.agda`) defines `TimeUnit` (`ns`/`╬╝s`/`ms`/`s`), `Timestamp (@0 u : TimeUnit)` with `tsValue : тДХ` projection, and unit-preserving operators `_тИ╕с╡Ч_`/`_тЙдс╡Ч_`/`_тЙдс╡Чс╡З_`/`_тЙбс╡Чс╡З_`/`_тИ╕тВЬтВЩ_` plus retraction lemmas `tsValue-mkTs`/`mkTs-tsValue`. MAlonzo strips the erased unit entirely: `newtype T_Timestamp_18 = C_mkTs_26 Integer` is the same runtime shape as the old `Timestamp = тДХ` alias, so there is zero hot-path cost (confirmed by benchmarks тАФ Frame Building numbers are at or above the 2026-04-08 post-fix baseline). Two Agda types `Timestamp ╬╝s` vs `Timestamp ms` are now distinct and cannot be mixed without an explicit conversion. `Protocol/FrameProcessor/Properties.agda` and `StreamState.agda` use a new `timestampтДХ : TimedFrame тЖТ тДХ` helper to unwrap at arithmetic/comparison boundaries (metric LTL operators, `checkMonotonic`, `updateCacheFromFrame`). `AletheiaFFI.hs` constructs timestamps via `AgdaTime.C_mkTs_26 (toInteger timestamp)` in all three FFI entry points (`aletheia_send_frame`, `aletheia_send_error`, `aletheia_send_remote`); MAlonzo renumbered the `TimedFrame`/`TraceEvent` constructor mangling to `C_constructor_32`/`C_Error_38`/`C_Remote_40` as a side-effect of the new runtime-relevant field. The unit is fixed at `╬╝s` across all bindings (C++ `std::chrono::microseconds`, Go `Timestamp{Microseconds int64}`, Python docstrings, the binary protocol wire format) тАФ the parameter exists for theorem parameterisation, in-source documentation, and future extensibility to higher-frequency buses. Total: 13 modified files (1 new, 12 edited тАФ `Trace/CANTrace.agda`, `Protocol/StreamState.agda`, `Protocol/Handlers.agda`, `Protocol/Response.agda`, `Protocol/ResponseFormat.agda`, `Protocol/FrameProcessor/Properties.agda`, `LTL/Coalgebra.agda`, `LTL/Semantics.agda`, `LTL/Semantics/MTL.agda`, `LTL/Adequacy.agda`, `LTL/Adequacy/Agreement.agda`, `LTL/Adequacy/WarmCache.agda`). 95 Agda modules total (was 94 + `Trace/Time.agda`). SignalCache `lastObserved : тДХ` intentionally left unchanged тАФ it is internal bookkeeping outside the 10.1 scope and refining it would touch 9 files and reopen `Cache/Properties.agda` proofs for no new dimensional-analysis benefit. All correctness gates green: Python 546 passing, C++ 5/5 ctest, Go -race + vet + gofmt clean, basedpyright 0/0/0, cabal build in 1m38s.

**Deferred non-blocker 11.1 тАФ in-source caution added (2026-04-08)** тАФ Following the Timestamp refinement, deferred item 11.1 (`mkPredTable`'s atom index refactored from `тДХ` to `Fin (length atoms)`, eliminating the proven-dead `nothing тЖТ Unknown` branch structurally) was re-analysed and confirmed deferred on performance grounds. MAlonzo compiles `Fin n` as a unary Peano chain (`data T_Fin_10 = C_zero_12 | C_suc_16 T_Fin_10`) тАФ each `Fin k` is k heap-allocated cells, each pattern match a heap dereference тАФ whereas the current `тДХ` index compiles via BUILTIN to Haskell `Integer` with native `eqInt`/`subInt`. Since `mkPredTable` runs per frame on the streaming loop and its returned closure is invoked by `stepL` for every Atomic cell, this is exactly the same class of hazard as the `Dec`-vs-`Bool` regression (commit `5aa345e`, 30тАУ65% throughput loss). A ~40-line comment block above `mkPredTable` in `src/Aletheia/Protocol/StreamState/Internals.agda:91` now documents the refactor option, the performance hazard, the structural cost (~8 files, four-valued `agreement` theorem shape change, FFI mangling re-verification), and the recommendation to leave it alone unless benchmarked first. `project_system_review_deferred.md` 11.1 updated with the hazard summary and pointer to the in-source caution. No runtime code change; `agda Aletheia/Protocol/StreamState/Internals.agda` clean.

**Deferred non-blockers 15.1/15.2 тАФ large Properties files split into per-topic submodules (2026-04-08)** тАФ Closes the last structural item from `project_system_review_deferred.md`. Both `Aletheia.CAN.Encoding.Properties` (1581 lines, 22 public theorems) and `Aletheia.Protocol.FrameProcessor.Properties` (1256 lines, 28+ public theorems) are now curated facades that re-export per-topic submodules via `open import X.Y public using (...)` blocks. **15.1**: `src/Aletheia/CAN/Encoding/Properties.agda` (1581L) тЖТ `Properties/Arithmetic.agda` (Layer 2 тДХтЖФтДд + Layer 3 тДдтЖФтДЪ algebraic bridge lemmas) + `Properties/Roundtrip.agda` (Layer 4 composition: signal-level `extract тИШ inject тЙб id` for unsigned/signed + `WellFormedSignal` record) + `Properties/Disjoint.agda` (bit preservation under disjoint injection, including mixed byte-order physical disjointness) + 78L facade. **15.2**: `src/Aletheia/Protocol/FrameProcessor/Properties.agda` (1256L) тЖТ `Properties/Step.agda` (223L, P1-P8 + P14-P15: state machine guards, `classifyStepResult`/`stepProperty`/`dispatchIterResult` characterisations, Streaming decomposition, Ack/Violation soundness + completeness) + `Properties/Cache.agda` (197L, P10-P13 + P23-P26: cache update decomposition + monotonicity / timestamp-bound preservation) + `Properties/Handlers.agda` (112L, P16-P22: FFI link properties + read-only handler state preservation) + `Properties/Bounded.agda` (625L, P9 `mkPredTable` faithfulness + P27 atom-index bound through `simplify`/`stepL`) + `Properties/Monotonic.agda` (209L, P28-P29: timestamp monotonicity enforcement at the step level + trace-level lift via `checkedFrames`/`HeadBounded` to `Trace.CANTrace.Monotonic`) + ~150L facade. Submodule dependency graph: `Handlers` imports `handleDataFrame-ack-sound` from `Step`; `Monotonic` imports `handleDataFrame-streaming` from `Step`; `Bounded` and `Cache` are leaf modules. The facades re-export every public name so external consumers import the same path unchanged тАФ `LTL/Adequacy/WarmCache.agda` still imports `AllBelow` and `mkPredTable-lookup` from the top-level `Aletheia.Protocol.FrameProcessor.Properties` path. Zero MAlonzo impact: neither facade is in `AletheiaFFI.hs`'s import graph, and the submodule path is what determines mangling (the facade is a pure source-level layer). Splitting buys faster IDE jump-to-definition, independent re-checking per layer, and removes the "one file with many abstraction levels" smell that AGENTS.md Category 15 flags. Total line count across FrameProcessor submodules + facade is 1516 (was 1256 monolithic) тАФ the overhead is facade headers and per-submodule imports, traded for navigation. Gates: Agda type-check clean (Monotonic uses qualified `Data.Nat.<с╡З` with local `where open import` blocks attached to `with eq` clauses, type-checked successfully), cabal build in 1m51s, Python 546 passing, C++ 5/5 ctest, Go -race + vet + gofmt clean. 95 Agda modules (was 88 тЖТ +5 FrameProcessor submodules + 3 Encoding submodules тИТ 1 monolithic Encoding тИТ 0 monolithic FrameProcessor; the monolithic files become facades, so net is +7 modules, but the count was already 95 pre-split).

**Deferred non-blocker 14.1 тАФ curated Main.agda public API (2026-04-08)** тАФ Closes deferred non-blocker 14.1 from `project_system_review_deferred.md`. `src/Aletheia/Main.agda` is now a curated public facade; the old two-line `open import Main.JSON public` / `open import Main.Binary public` is replaced with explicit `using (...)` lists grouped into seven sections (FFI entry points; state machine; command dispatch; frame/trace/DLC types; error types and inspection; JSON and response formatting). The two constructors are re-exported as `ResponseError` and `TraceError`, leaving the canonical `Error` name free for the top-level sum type. `src/Aletheia/Main/JSON.agda` cleanup: the helpers `wrapJSON`, `tryParseCommand`, `dispatchCommand`, `handleParsedJSON` are now wrapped in a `private` block (matching `Main/Binary.agda`); `processJSONLine` stays public with its NOINLINE pragma. MAlonzo numbering is unchanged тАФ `d_processJSONLine_64` still exists with the same number and `AletheiaFFI.hs` continues to reference it without modification; MAlonzo compiles private Agda definitions to numbered Haskell symbols regardless of visibility, so the private rewrite is a pure source-level cleanup with zero effect on the FFI name contract. 2 files touched. **Deferred non-blocker ┬з12.1 тАФ JSONParser enforces PhysicallyValid (2026-04-08)** тАФ Closes the last proof-breadth item in `project_system_review_deferred.md`. `DBC/JSONParser.agda` now enforces `PhysicallyValid` at parse time via a `physicalGate` helper: LittleEndian passes through (LE signals trivially satisfy `pv-LE`), BigEndian runs three nested `ifс╡А` checks (`1 тЙдс╡З bl`, `csb + bl тИ╕ 1 <с╡З frameBytes * 8`, `bl тИ╕ 1 тЙдс╡З csb`), each failed check emitting a distinct `ParseError`. `parse-wellformed` is strengthened from `WellFormedDBC` to `WellFormedDBCRT`, which lifts the conditional `parse-format-parse-given-PV` theorem to the unconditional `parse-format-parse : тИА j d тЖТ parseDBCWithErrors j тЙб injтВВ d тЖТ parseDBCWithErrors (formatDBC d) тЙб parseDBCWithErrors j`. `PhysicallyValid` refactored from a 4-field record to a 2-constructor data type in `Formatter/WellFormed.agda` (`pv-LE` for LE signals, `pv-BE` carrying the three bound proofs for BE); the old record form rejected `startBit = 0` LE signals via an over-strong `msb-ge-len` constraint. `signal-roundtrip-go` in `Formatter/SignalRoundtrip.agda` pattern-matches on `pv-BE`/`pv-LE` and the BE clauses rewrite with `тЙдтЖТтЙдс╡З-true`/`<тЖТ<с╡З-true` to discharge the gate's nested `ifс╡А` branches. New ParseError variants: `SignalBitLengthZero`, `SignalOverflowsFrame тДХ тДХ тДХ`, `SignalMSBBelowBitLength тДХ тДХ`, with error codes `parse_signal_bit_length_zero`, `parse_signal_overflows_frame`, `parse_signal_msb_below_bit_length`; total error code count 41 тЖТ 44. Mirrors added to Python `aletheia/protocols.py`, C++ `error.hpp` + `json_parse.cpp`, Go `error.go`. `parseSignalFields-wf` split into a `postPresence-wf` helper that takes the byte order explicitly (the with-chain on `physicalGate` is stuck on `bo` otherwise); companion `parseSignalFields-pv` returns `PhysicallyValid frameBytes sig`. Chain: `parseSignalFields-pv` тЖТ `parseSignal-pv` тЖТ `parseSignalList-pv` тЖТ `parseMessageBody-pv` тЖТ `parseMessage-pv` тЖТ `parseMessageList-pv` (returns `All WellFormedMessageRT msgs` by combining `parseMessage-wf` and `parseMessage-pv` at each cons step). Behaviour change: `test_big_endian_signal_exceeds_dlc` in `python/tests/test_dbc_validator.py` now asserts the BE overflow is caught at parse time (`parse_signal_overflows_frame`) rather than downstream by the validator's `signal_exceeds_dlc` тАФ the validator's BE overflow check is now provably redundant for parser-validated DBCs. Gates: Cabal build 1m36s (all 218 MAlonzo modules clean, `libaletheia-ffi.so` rebuilt); Python 546 passing; basedpyright 0/0/0; pylint 9.97/10; C++ 5/5 ctest; Go -race + vet + gofmt clean. Benchmarks: all within ┬▒5% of 2026-04-08 post-fix baseline тАФ `physicalGate` runs only at parse time (one-shot DBC load), not on the streaming hot path, so no throughput impact.

**Post-commit benchmark-driven fix (2026-04-08)** тАФ Frame-building throughput regression (30тАУ65% across all 3 bindings, CAN-FD worst at -64%) initially misdiagnosed as the D1+D2+D3 handler dedup in `Protocol/Handlers.agda`. `git worktree` bisection pinpointed commit `5aa345e` as the actual root cause: it replaced the O(1) `rangesOverlap` in `BatchFrameBuilding.hasOverlaps` with the Dec-valued `physicallyDisjoint?`, whose nested `allBounded` quantifier allocates `Dec` proof terms per bit-pair per frame тАФ MAlonzo `Integer`-boxing on those allocations dominates the hot path. The binary FFI benchmark path (`processBuildFrameBin` тЖТ `buildFrameByIndex`) bypasses `Handlers.agda` entirely, which is why D1+D2+D3 could not have been responsible. Fix: Bool-valued `signalsPhysicallyOverlapс╡З` fast path in `DBC/Properties.agda` with precomputed per-signal bit lists hoisted out of the O(m┬▓) pair loop, plus equivalence proofs `physicallyOverlapс╡З-sound` / `physicallyOverlapс╡З-complete` establishing `signalsPhysicallyOverlapс╡З тЙб false тЗФ PhysicallyDisjoint`. Supporting lemmas: `bitsMemberс╡З-false-absent`, `bitsIntersectс╡З-false-disjoint`, `buildPhysicalBits-тИИ`, `signalPhysicalBits-тИИ`, `buildPhysicalBits-тИИтЖТoffset`, `signalPhysicalBits-тИИтЖТoffset`, `bitsMemberс╡З-trueтЖТтИИ`, `bitsIntersectс╡З-trueтЖТwitness`. The fast path is as trustworthy as the Dec-valued check; both are provably equivalent. Recovery: CAN 2.0B Frame Building +23тАУ37% and CAN-FD Frame Building +107тАУ147% vs the regression state. AGENTS.md Category 16 updated with the Dec-vs-Bool cost-model lesson; `feedback_hot_path_refactor_benchmark.md` updated with the correct diagnosis; `project_frame_building_regression_2026_04_07.md` marked RESOLVED.

**Path G тАФ three-valued Kleene FinalVerdict (2026-04-09)** тАФ Closes the soundness-but-user-surprising gap where `Always(p)` on a trace that never observes `p`'s signal would operationally yield `Fails` at end-of-stream, while the denotational semantics `тЯж Always (Atomic p) тЯз ╧Г` says Unknown. Path G adds an `Unsure : String тЖТ FinalVerdict` constructor to `Aletheia.LTL.Incremental.FinalVerdict`, refactors `finalizeL` in `LTL/Coalgebra.agda` to three-valued Kleene K3 logic (Atomic тЖТ Unsure, Not/And/Or combine via K3 truth tables with Fails as тКе and Holds as тКд), and adds a new `finalizesFails : LTLProc тЖТ Bool` helper in `LTL/Simplify.agda` as the guarded companion to `finalizesHolds` тАФ the `Or ╧Ж (Eventually ╧И) тЖТ Eventually ╧И` absorption now requires `finalizesFails ╧Ж = true` (Unsure alone does not justify collapsing to Fails). Adequacy: `verdictToSV` maps Unsure тЖТ Unknown, and `finalize-empty-equiv` in `LTL/Coalgebra/Properties.agda` is updated so that the empty-trace Atomic case resolves to Unknown on both sides. `LTL/Semantics.agda` denotation of `Atomic p` on empty trace is now `Unknown` (matching the operational result). `LTL/SimplifySound.agda` soundness lemmas for empty-trace And/Or cases are rewritten to delegate to per-verdict helpers `runL-X-[] a b (finalizeL a) (finalizeL b) refl refl hyp`, working around Agda's limitation where nested `with finalizeL a | finalizeL b` scrutinee abstraction does not partially evaluate past intermediate `refl` rewrites тАФ the helper form takes the two FinalVerdicts as explicit parameters and discharges the K3 combination algebraically. `LTL/Semantics/MTL.agda` four-valued metric combinators updated with Unsure absorption lemmas. **Protocol layer**: `Protocol/Response.agda` adds an `Unresolved` `PropertyResult` constructor mirroring `Violation` (`property_index`, `reason` fields); `Protocol/Handlers.agda` dispatch converts `FinalVerdict.Unsure r` into `Unresolved`; `Protocol/ResponseFormat.agda` emits `"status": "unresolved"` in the JSON results array. **Bindings**: Python `protocols.py` adds `"unresolved"` to the `status` Literal and `_client.py _parse_finalization_results` handles the new branch; `cli.py` prints a separate `Unresolved` section in `check` output and the JSON summary now carries `total_unresolved`/`unresolved` fields with `status тИИ {"violations", "unresolved", "pass"}`. C++ `response.hpp` adds `Verdict::Unresolved`, `json_parse.cpp parse_stream_result` maps `"unresolved"` тЖТ `Verdict::Unresolved`, `client.cpp end_stream` enriches both Fails and Unresolved and logs them separately. Go `result.go` adds `Unresolved` to the `Verdict` iota with `.String() = "unresolved"`, `json.go parsePropertyResult` maps the JSON string, `client.go EndStream` handles both via a switch. Tests: `python/tests/test_eos_finalization.py` updated тАФ 4 tests (`test_changed_by_never_one_frame`, `test_always_never_observed_one_frame`, `test_always_never_observed_many_frames`, `test_eventually_never_observed_is_consistent`) were pinning the pre-Path-G Fails/vacuous-Holds behaviour and now assert `"unresolved"`; the class docstring rewrites the trace walk in K3 terms (`Unsure тИз Holds = Unsure`, `Unsure тИи Fails = Unsure`). New `test_end_stream_unresolved_verdict` in `test_unified_client.py`, `TestStreamingLTL_Unresolved` in `go/aletheia/stream_test.go`, third `"unresolved"` result entry in the `parse_stream_result complete` C++ Catch2 test, Go `TestVerdictString`'s Unresolved branch, C++ `static_asserts` for `Verdict::Unresolved` distinctness. **Drive-by**: 154 pre-existing clang-format violations across `cpp/include/aletheia/backend.hpp`, `cpp/src/{backend,client,enrich,ffi_backend,json_parse}.cpp`, and `cpp/tests/integration_tests.cpp` fixed via `clang-format -i` (one-line `if (s == "...") return тАж;` statements violating `AllowShortIfStatementsOnASingleLine: Never`); this is an unrelated baseline cleanup triggered by the tool gate per `feedback_fix_tool_gate_violations.md`. Also caught a lurking bug from the earlier Path G protocol commit: `cpp/src/json_parse.cpp parse_stream_result` had the enum and test updated but the parser switch still threw `"Unknown verdict status: unresolved"` тАФ the third test entry exposed it. Gates: Agda type-check clean, cabal shake build in 1m33s (218 MAlonzo modules), Python 553 passing, basedpyright 0/0/0, pylint 10.00/10, C++ 5/5 ctest (142 unit + 14 integration + 33 YAML + 47 Excel), clang-format clean, Go 251 passing with `-race`, go vet + gofmt clean. 11 Agda files modified (no new modules); 103 Agda modules total, all `--safe --without-K`.

**Performance** (canonical source тАФ other docs may round or summarize these numbers):

*Benchmarks: 10,000 frames ├Ч 5 runs, AMD Ryzen 9 5950X, Linux 6.6 (WSL2). C++ g++-15 -O3, Go 1.26.1, Python 3.13.12.*

| Benchmark | C++ (fps) | Go (fps) | Python (fps) | Measured |
|---|---:|---:|---:|---|
| CAN 2.0B: Stream LTL (2 props) | **109,345** | 97,082 | 70,917 | 2026-04-06 |
| CAN 2.0B: Signal Extraction | **212,857** | 166,527 | 87,424 | 2026-04-06 |
| CAN 2.0B: Frame BuildingтАа | **76,469** | 71,692 | 55,093 | 2026-04-06 |
| CAN-FD: Stream LTL (3 props) | **48,248** | 47,516 | 34,737 | 2026-04-06 |
| CAN-FD: Signal Extraction | **14,930** | 14,493 | 12,143 | 2026-04-06 |
| CAN-FD: Frame BuildingтАа | **20,567** | 20,052 | 17,830 | 2026-04-06 |

тАа Frame Building rows have an additional post-fix 2026-04-08 measurement documented in the note immediately below the table; those numbers are not the canonical ones and are deliberately not substituted here.

> **Frame Building regression resolved (2026-04-08).** An earlier 30тАУ65% regression on Frame Building rows (commit `5aa345e`, introduced by the `physicallyDisjoint?` Dec-valued check in `BatchFrameBuilding.hasOverlaps`) was traced via `git worktree` bisection and fixed by a Bool-valued fast path with formal equivalence proofs in `DBC/Properties.agda` (`signalsPhysicallyOverlapс╡З`, `physicallyOverlapс╡З-sound`, `physicallyOverlapс╡З-complete`). Per-signal physical bit lists are precomputed once in `hasOverlaps` and the O(m┬▓) pair loop runs over cached lists with primitive тДХ equality тАФ no `Dec` allocations on the hot path. See `project_frame_building_regression_2026_04_07.md` and AGENTS.md Category 16 for the cost-model lesson. The canonical numbers above still reflect the 2026-04-06 steady state; post-fix measurements (10000 frames ├Ч 5 runs, 2026-04-08) show Frame Building at C++ 58,712 / Go 65,106 / Python 47,789 (CAN 2.0B) and C++ 15,226 / Go 17,181 / Python 14,858 (CAN-FD) тАФ a full +107тАУ147% recovery on CAN-FD vs the regression state. The remaining gap (~10тАУ25%) vs canonical reflects system noise plus residual list-representation overhead; further optimization is not blocked.

> **Note on C++ vs Go on Frame Building.** Frame Building is the only benchmark where Go can overtake C++, and the 2026-04-08 run does show Go +11% on CAN 2.0B and +13% on CAN-FD. This is not a C++ vs Go performance truth тАФ it is benchmark geometry. Frame Building does the *least* Agda work per call and the *most* binding-side work, so per-call glibc `malloc` for the three scratch `std::vector`s in `AletheiaClient::build_frame` plus `std::unordered_map<SignalKey, uint32>` lookups become visible relative to Go's per-P bump allocator and built-in map. Stream LTL and Signal Extraction remain clearly C++-dominant. Future C++ optimizations (thread-local scratch buffers, small-vector, `ankerl::unordered_dense` / `absl::flat_hash_map`) would likely recapture the Frame Building lead but are not scheduled. See `project_cpp_vs_go_frame_building.md` for details.

- Build time: 0.26s (no-op), ~11s (incremental)
- Per-frame latency: ~9 us (CAN 2.0B streaming, C++)
- Memory: O(1) verified (1.08x growth across 100x trace increase)
- **Binary FFI**: All hot-path operations use binary FFI (no JSON parsing): `aletheia_send_frame` (streaming), `aletheia_extract_signals_bin`, `aletheia_build_frame_bin`, `aletheia_update_frame_bin`. All three bindings call the binary endpoints directly.
- **Single-threaded runtime**: Deployable to minimal containers (1 vCPU) with headroom over a 500 kbit/s CAN bus (~4,000 frames/sec). CAN-FD at 5 Mbit/s requires ~6,000 fps тАФ all operations exceed this across all bindings (minimum: 12,143 fps Python CAN-FD extraction, 2x headroom).
- **Multi-bus scaling**: Each `AletheiaClient` has independent state (`StablePtr`). Multiple Python threads can monitor separate CAN buses in parallel. ctypes releases the GIL during FFI calls. For N buses on N vCPUs, pass `-N` to `hs_init` for parallel GHC capabilities.

**Verification**:
- All 246 of 247 Agda modules use `--safe --without-K` (4 also use `--no-main`; 1 allowlisted `--without-K`-only `Substrate.Unsafe` hosts the two stdlib-equivalent `String тЖФ List Char` bridging axioms + the universal `parseText (formatText d) тЙб injтВВ d` consumer)
- Zero postulates in production code
- All provable correctness properties proven (LTL adequacy, DBC validation, signal roundtrip, frame processing, predicate table, signal cache, response formatting, initial state, metric operator window bounds)
- **Pipeline soundness proven**: 8 unsound absorption rules removed, 4 remaining guarded with `finalizesHolds`, 2 structural idempotency rules added. `absorb-runL`, `simplify-runL`, `pipeline-adequate`, `production-adequate` all proven in `Adequacy/Pipeline.agda`
- **All verification suites green**: Python (basedpyright 0 errors, pylint 10.00/10), C++ (clang-format clean, clang-tidy clean, all ctest suites pass), Go (go test -race, go vet, gofmt all clean)

### Phase 6: Extensions & New Protocols (Planned)

**Scope**: Binding feature gaps, dependency cleanup, and automotive Ethernet support.  Goal-set refreshed 2026-05-07 after R17 fully closed.

**Binding feature gaps** (closed en route тАФ kept for archaeology):
- ~~DBC `.dbc` text file parsing for C++ and Go~~ тЬЕ Closed by Track B.3 2026-05-03 (`bca99f2`).
- ~~Go multiplexing query helpers~~ тЬЕ Closed by Track B.2 audit 2026-04-XX (helpers were already shipped client-side).

**Binding feature gaps** (active):
- **CLI parity for C++/Go (stretch goal, 2026-05-07)** тАФ Python ships `python -m aletheia` with six subcommands: `check` / `validate` / `extract` / `signals` / `format-dbc` / `mux-query`.  C++ and Go are currently `not_applicable` in the FEATURE_MATRIX with reason "library bindings; CLI tools are a host-application concern."  Stretch-goal flip: rebuild the same subcommand surface in each language as a thin host binary dispatching to the existing client API.  Estimate ~300-500 LOC per language (CLI is glue, not parser, so the estimate is honest).  No Agda or FFI changes.  Drives a `cli` matrix row flip from `not_applicable` to `planned` ├Ч 2.

**Toolchain upgrades**:
- Upgrade `basedpyright` and `pylint` to the latest stable releases, re-verify the 0/0/0 + 10.00/10 gates on the updated versions, and bump the upper pins in `python/pyproject.toml` (`basedpyright>=1.0,<2`, `pylint>=3.0,<4`) accordingly.

**LGPL contingency** (refreshed 2026-05-07):
- ~~cantools (transitively LGPL via python-can)~~ тЬЕ Closed by Track B.3.g (`2daa2fb`).  Verified Agda DBC text parser replaces it.
- **python-can replacement (Phase 6 goal)** тАФ `python/aletheia/can_log.py:22` imports `python-can` for ASC/BLF/MF4/etc. log file readers; declared as optional `can = ["python-can>=4.0"]` extra in `pyproject.toml:58`.  **Estimate is open, not "~300 LOC"**: per project rule "parsers are Agda + proof" (`feedback_parsers_are_agda_with_proof.md`), each log format goes through the verified kernel тАФ Agda implementation + roundtrip proof + binding wire layer per format (ASC text, BLF binary; MF4 deferred to `asammdf` BSD-3 if needed).  Track B.3 (DBC text parser) is the closest precedent: ~6 weeks of Agda + universal roundtrip theorem.  The 2026-03-22 ~300 LOC memo was based on a Python glue assumption that is invalid for this project.
- **GHC `--bignum=native` rebuild (Phase 6 goal)** тАФ `libgmp` (LGPL-3.0) currently links into `libaletheia-ffi.so` because GHC defaults to `integer-gmp`.  Replacement: rebuild GHC with `--bignum=native` (BSD-3, pure Haskell).  **Deliverable is a step-by-step + tested procedure**, not just a config flip тАФ script + verified commands on a clean machine, with before/after FFI .so hash + benchmark snapshot to confirm no regression.  Lives in `docs/development/` alongside BUILDING.md.

**SOME/IP support**:
- Extend Aletheia to automotive Ethernet via SOME/IP (Scalable service-Oriented MiddlewarE over IP)
- SOME/IP is fundamentally different from CAN: service-oriented rather than signal-based, with a 16-byte header and variable structured payloads
- Requires new frame model, extraction logic, and LTL atomic predicates (service-level: response timing, subscription freshness, method sequencing)
- Existing LTL engine is reusable; also covers CAN-over-Ethernet (DoIP/ISO 13400)

**Status**: Not started.  Goal-set locked 2026-05-07; no commitments to a phase ordering yet.
